<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Personality">Personality</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FKrieg%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D4&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>Krieg showcases the typical attributes of a militant leader, favoring cruel and oppressive tendencies using a huge arsenal of weapons and overwhelming odds. He is incapable of any sense of honor nor can he be sympathetic for anyone.
</p>
<table class="noprint" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" border="0" style="width:100%; clear:both;">
</table><table class="noprint" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" border="0" align="center" style="background:none; text-align:center;">
 <tbody><tr>
  <td style="vertical-align:top; font-size:3em; color:#88B7FD; font-family:&#39;Times New Roman&#39;,serif; font-weight:bold; padding:.3em 0em 0em 0em; text-shadow: 1px -1px gray;">“</td>
  <td style="padding:1em 1em; font-family:&#39;Times New Roman&#39;,serif;; font-style:italic; font-size:medium; color:inherit;">You know that above all I detest sentimental tripe like "honor" and "mercy." This is war! All that matters is victory! 
</td>
  <td style="vertical-align:bottom; font-size:3em; color:#88B7FD; font-family:&#39;Times New Roman&#39;,serif; font-weight:bold; padding-bottom:0em; padding-left:0em; padding-right:0em; text-shadow: -1px 1px gray;">”</td>
 </tr>
</tbody></table>
<table style="padding-right: 2%; font-size:80%; text-align:right; width:100%;">
 <tbody><tr valign="top">
  <td><cite style="font-family:&#39;Arial&#39;,sans-serif;">—&#160;Krieg's attitude towards battle in the anime.<sup id="cite_ref-10" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-10">&#91;10&#93;</a></sup></cite>
  </td>
 </tr>
</tbody></table>

<p><br />
Krieg is characterized by cruelty, dishonesty, and arrogance. He is confident in his own superiority, despite any failures he might experience, and believes wholeheartedly that his armada and arsenal of weapons can overcome any foe. Even in the face of his obvious inferiority, Krieg refused to accept or learn from his mistake, instead turning to underhanded methods to get by and believing that there was some sort of trick to overcoming such foes. Witnessing <a href="/wiki/Dracule_Mihawk" title="Dracule Mihawk">Dracule Mihawk</a>'s devastatingly powerful swordsmanship, Krieg accused him of simply having a <a href="/wiki/Devil_Fruit" title="Devil Fruit">Devil Fruit</a> power. Krieg has also proven to be very hypocritical as he chastises his crew for taking offense to Luffy calling them weak saying only a weakling is offended by words, but becomes angered himself when Luffy directly says he doesn't have what it takes to be <a href="/wiki/King_of_the_Pirates" class="mw-redirect" title="King of the Pirates">King of the Pirates</a>.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/b/b3/Krieg_Angry.png/revision/latest?cb=20221124050024" class="image"><img alt="Krieg Angry" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="158" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Krieg Angry.png" data-image-key="Krieg_Angry.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/b/b3/Krieg_Angry.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20221124050024" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/b/b3/Krieg_Angry.png/revision/latest?cb=20221124050024" class="image"><img alt="Krieg Angry" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/b/b3/Krieg_Angry.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20221124050024" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="158" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Krieg Angry.png" data-image-key="Krieg_Angry.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/b/b3/Krieg_Angry.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20221124050024" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Krieg_Angry.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Krieg when angered.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>However, his constant victories and reliance on weapons and odds made him overconfident. His <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/superiority_complex" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:superiority complex">superiority complex</a> makes it very easy for him to lose his temper if his orders are not fulfilled, usually taking it out on his subordinates. This led to his failed attempt to conquer the Grand Line, believing his reputation built on sheer numbers and military weapons were enough to get him by; he suffered an utter defeat when Mihawk almost completely annihilated his entire fleet.
</p><p>Krieg lives up to his nickname, "Foul Play", as he believes in winning above all else, and will stoop to any level to achieve it. An example of this was flying a white flag of surrender and posing as Marines to get the drop on them. Due to his philosophy, he considers concepts like pride and sympathy to be pathetic, and will go to any lengths to win, resulting in his willingness to kill subordinates who display such emotions, disregarding their loyalty and strength. He has no attachments to either his crew or his ships, immediately preparing to rebuild his fleet with the various pirate crews scattered in East Blue instead of mourning the loss of his previous one, and plotting to sink his own flagship to get a new one due to the damage it has incurred. His lack of morale led him to ungratefully assault the Baratie when they gave food to him and his starving crew, intending to take over their ship and kill all the chefs who remained. Intolerant of failure and loss, Krieg lost all hold on his composure when Luffy defeated him, and stood up to demand a rematch despite his critical injuries.
</p><p>Krieg keeps his crew together using fear. Despite how mad and ridiculous some of his orders may seem, his crew will follow them out of fear of death, which is another factor that limits their strength. Overall, he rules his crew with draconian might and expects utter obedience for his overbearing demands. However, some members, like <a href="/wiki/Gin" title="Gin">Gin</a>, have genuine respect for Krieg, while <a href="/wiki/Pearl" title="Pearl">Pearl</a> shares the belief trickery is the key to victory and survival.
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Relationships">Relationships</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FKrieg%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D5&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Crew">Crew</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FKrieg%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D6&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Despite his cruel tendencies, Krieg is pragmatic enough to realize that he needs a crew to support him. He thus made sure they were fed to regain their full strength after Mihawk's onslaught. However, Krieg does not care for his crew and rules over them with fear and anyone who opposes him is typically punished with death. He is very proud of his rank as captain, and gets very mad when someone disobeys him, or even hesitates to carry out his orders, as he believes it is their duty to obey him unquestionably.<sup id="cite_ref-11" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-11">&#91;11&#93;</a></sup> During the attack on the Baratie, Krieg expressed his desire to conquer the Baratie and go back to the Grand Line. This shocked the crew because they were feeling gratitude towards the chefs and did not want to go back to that pirate graveyard, but they complied out of fear of their captain and that one member was shot for voicing his opinion.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Gin">Gin</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FKrieg%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D7&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p><a href="/wiki/Gin" title="Gin">Gin</a> is fiercely loyal to Krieg, carrying out whatever orders he may be given from him, no matter how inhumanly brutal or ruthless they may be, without protest or hesitation, thus earning himself the alias of "Gin the Demon Man". This is partly due to a great fear of Krieg, which is evidenced when he obeyed his orders to throw away his gas mask and breathe the deadly MH5 poison gas because he feared Krieg's wrath for disobeying more than death itself. After Krieg was defeated by Luffy, the Pirate Admiral went on an insane rampage, refusing to acknowledge defeat, but Gin punched him in the stomach, knocking the man out, stating that they must admit defeat and start over. He then carried away Krieg and the crew in a small boat given by Baratie.
</p><p>Despite previously dismissing Gin from the crew for being merciful, he seemed to have retracted the dismissal when the two of them were seen side-by-side on <a href="/wiki/Hachinosu" title="Hachinosu">Hachinosu</a> two years later.<sup id="cite_ref-c1117_12-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c1117-12">&#91;12&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Pearl">Pearl</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FKrieg%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D8&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p><a href="/wiki/Pearl" title="Pearl">Pearl</a>, despite his overconfidence in his own so-called unbreakable defense, also acknowledged his captain, but unlike Gin, Pearl does not have a sense of honor, instead falling in the lines of Krieg's ideology of foul play being essential in victory and survival.
</p><p>For his part, Krieg considers Pearl useful but nevertheless expendable, and is particularly wary of his "Fire Pearl" technique. When Pearl was panicked by a small, accidental injury at the <a href="/wiki/Baratie" title="Baratie">Baratie</a> and began igniting it, Krieg immediately tried to calm him; once this failed, Krieg showed no qualms about "sinking" Pearl (and Sanji) with his Morningstar in order to keep the Baratie intact for his own plans.<sup id="cite_ref-c55_13-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c55-13">&#91;13&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Enemies">Enemies</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FKrieg%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D9&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Dracule_Mihawk">Dracule Mihawk</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FKrieg%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D10&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Mihawk also became an enemy of Krieg, destroying Krieg's entire fleet when he attempted to conquer the Grand Line. However, Mihawk claims he only attacked the crew to kill time and did not consider Krieg a threat. Upon sighting Mihawk, Krieg's anger led him to attack Mihawk, despite having witnessed <a href="/wiki/Roronoa_Zoro" title="Roronoa Zoro">Zoro</a>'s defeat and his own ship having been sliced apart. Mihawk did not even bother to retaliate, instead merely slashing Krieg's ship again and departing during the distraction.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Marines">Marines</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FKrieg%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D11&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>As a famous pirate with a bounty on his head, Krieg is an enemy of the marines. In the past, he also killed a marine captain and took over his ship to start his pirate career.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Baratie">Baratie</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FKrieg%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D12&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Krieg saw the value of stealing the harmless looking restaurant as a ploy for his pirate crew. However, at first, Krieg lied by telling that he only wanted food for him and his men. When Krieg recovered his strength, he revealed his intentions to steal the Baratie for his new flagship, rebuild his armada with other pirate crews found littered within the sea, and then return to the Grand Line with <a href="/wiki/Zeff" title="Zeff">Zeff</a>'s logbook as a guide. The chefs fought against the revived Krieg’s crew to maintain their restaurant.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Straw_Hat_Pirates">Straw Hat Pirates</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FKrieg%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D13&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Krieg became an enemy of <a href="/wiki/Monkey_D._Luffy" title="Monkey D. Luffy">Monkey D. Luffy</a> for his desire to take the Baratie as well as his ambition to become the pirate king. Krieg was blinded by his arrogance and Luffy and his crew's seemingly harmless looks, and mocked Luffy for his statements. After witnessing the <a href="/wiki/Roronoa_Zoro" title="Roronoa Zoro">"Pirate Hunter" Zoro</a> and Luffy's <a href="/wiki/Gomu_Gomu_no_Mi" title="Gomu Gomu no Mi">Devil Fruit powers</a>, Krieg came to believe that Luffy would just be another pirate in the Grand Line, as the place was filled with ability users like him, and tried to take full advantage of Luffy's weakness of the ocean during their battle. After a long battle, Luffy managed to defeat Krieg, but even after the battle was over, Krieg unconsciously gets up and demanded to continue the battle, only to be knocked down by Gin.
</p><p>Also, despite the fact that <a href="/wiki/Sanji" title="Sanji">Sanji</a> (who was not part of the crew at the time) was willing to help Krieg and his hungry men, when he regained his strength, Krieg immediately attacked him. He also ordered Gin to kill him.
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Abilities_and_Powers">Abilities and Powers</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FKrieg%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D14&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>Krieg was considered (in military strength) the most powerful pirate in the East Blue and had a terrible reputation for his devious and deceptive tactics in piracy. Although Krieg had a lower bounty than <a href="/wiki/Arlong" title="Arlong">Arlong</a> (especially with the fish-man bribing the Marines to keep it low),<sup id="cite_ref-14" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-14">&#91;14&#93;</a></sup> his fleet of 50 ships and over 5,000 pirates,<sup id="cite_ref-c48_15-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c48-15">&#91;15&#93;</a></sup> combined with active pillaging, forced the <a href="/wiki/Marines" title="Marines">Marines</a> to view Krieg as a greater threat in East Blue.<sup id="cite_ref-c45_1-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c45-1">&#91;1&#93;</a></sup> Despite this, however, it was commented by <a href="/wiki/Monkey_D._Luffy" title="Monkey D. Luffy">Luffy</a> that Krieg's <a href="/wiki/Fleet" title="Fleet">fleet</a> was not all that powerful. They were just using sheer numbers alone to overwhelm their opponents.<sup id="cite_ref-16" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-16">&#91;16&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Physical_Abilities">Physical Abilities</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FKrieg%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D15&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Krieg also claimed to be the strongest man in the world, and while this is clearly a vast overestimation on his part, he is certainly formidable in physical combat, possessing massive physical strength. He could break Gin's arm with his grip, defend against cannonballs without moving an inch, and easily lift and throw the <a href="/wiki/Sabagashira_I" title="Sabagashira I">Sabagashira I</a> a far distance into the Baratie restaurant with a single hand. He can also lift the one-ton Great Battle Spear single-handedly and swing it around freely while wearing his golden wootz armor.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Master_Strategist">Master Strategist</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FKrieg%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D16&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Krieg is also a sound tactician and expert strategist, realizing the material value of his subordinates and requiring them to be at perfect health, as well as using decoys and disguises to avoid unnecessary battles (such as disguising his flagship as a Marine vessel to enter village harbors easily, or dressing up his first-mate as himself to distract pursuers). His dishonest and unethical behavior, despite showing his lack of honesty, is a testament of his strategic aptitude. His plan to steal Baratie as a suitable replacement for his damaged ship due to its ridiculous and non-threatening appearance would prove crucial for his future pirate ambitions. He also has knowledge of <a href="/wiki/Devil_Fruit" title="Devil Fruit">Devil Fruits</a>, as shown when he witnessed Luffy's ability to stretch and planned to throw him into the water in order to disable him, noting that the Grand Line is supposed to be filled with such people. However, Krieg's most potent weapon has always been his talent for trickery, which seemed to know no bounds. He lies and pretends to beg for mercy before striking when his opponents lower their guards. His methods have earned him the nickname "Foul Play".
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Weapons">Weapons</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FKrieg%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D17&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/9/94/Kaen_Hosha.png/revision/latest?cb=20230524230625" class="image"><img alt="Kaen Hosha" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="135" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Kaen Hosha.png" data-image-key="Kaen_Hosha.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/9/94/Kaen_Hosha.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20230524230625" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/9/94/Kaen_Hosha.png/revision/latest?cb=20230524230625" class="image"><img alt="Kaen Hosha" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/9/94/Kaen_Hosha.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20230524230625" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="135" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Kaen Hosha.png" data-image-key="Kaen_Hosha.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/9/94/Kaen_Hosha.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20230524230625" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Kaen_Hosha.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Krieg using "Kaen Hosha"</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Krieg's fighting style is almost exclusively tied to his huge arsenal of weapons. True to his "Foul Play" moniker, he keeps most of these weapons hidden or otherwise inconspicuous until the exact moment he deploys them, counting on not only raw firepower but the element of surprise to overwhelm his foes.<sup id="cite_ref-c47_17-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c47-17">&#91;17&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>(Accordingly, Krieg "names" very few of his attacks out loud; most of his weapons are identified by onlookers, particularly his crew.)
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Armor">Armor</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FKrieg%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D18&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>The centerpiece of Krieg's arsenal is his <b><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Wootz_steel" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Wootz steel">Wootz steel</a> armor</b><span style="font-weight: normal"> (<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja">ウーツ鋼の鎧</span><span class="t_nihongo_comma">,</span> <i><span class="t_nihongo_romaji">Ūtsu-Kō no Yoroi</span></i><span class="t_nihongo_help"><sup><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Help:Japanese" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Help:Japanese"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color:#00e;font:bold 80% sans-serif;text-decoration:none;padding:0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup></span>)</span>, bright gold in color. Reputedly—though, as <a href="/wiki/Monkey_D._Luffy" title="Monkey D. Luffy">Luffy</a> eventually proved, not totally—indestructible, its carapace can withstand a point-blank <a href="/wiki/Firearm#Bazookas" title="Firearm">bazooka</a> shot without any hint of damage to either the exterior or Krieg himself.<sup id="cite_ref-c47_17-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c47-17">&#91;17&#93;</a></sup> At the same time, it is flexible enough to permit Krieg considerable freedom of movement.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/5/5f/Dangan.png/revision/latest?cb=20230103223924" class="image"><img alt="Dangan" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="158" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Dangan.png" data-image-key="Dangan.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/5/5f/Dangan.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230103223924" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/5/5f/Dangan.png/revision/latest?cb=20230103223924" class="image"><img alt="Dangan" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/5/5f/Dangan.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230103223924" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="158" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Dangan.png" data-image-key="Dangan.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/5/5f/Dangan.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230103223924" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Dangan.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Krieg's armor, with guns fully unveiled.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Many of Krieg's weapons are directly built into this armor, chief amongst them a set of ten <a href="/wiki/Firearm" title="Firearm">gun-barrels</a>—two beneath each shoulder-plate, and three beneath each of the carapace's waist-flaps. Through unknown mechanisms, Krieg can fire all of these in a single motion, allowing him to gun down dozens of enemies within seconds.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/0/01/Needle_Machine_Gun.png/revision/latest?cb=20230518230731" class="image"><img alt="Needle Machine Gun" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="158" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Needle Machine Gun.png" data-image-key="Needle_Machine_Gun.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/0/01/Needle_Machine_Gun.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230518230731" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/0/01/Needle_Machine_Gun.png/revision/latest?cb=20230518230731" class="image"><img alt="Needle Machine Gun" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/0/01/Needle_Machine_Gun.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230518230731" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="158" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Needle Machine Gun.png" data-image-key="Needle_Machine_Gun.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/0/01/Needle_Machine_Gun.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230518230731" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Needle_Machine_Gun.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Needle Machine Gun</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Each of the shoulder-plates can be removed and used as bludgeons to augment Krieg's already-powerful punches. In addition, the left plate holds many projectile launchers:
</p>
<ul><li>A dozen along the rim, meant to fire belt-fed spears in a <a href="/wiki/Firearm#Gatling_gun" title="Firearm">Gatling gun</a>-like fashion.</li>
<li>A central one, positioned under the <a href="/wiki/Jolly_Roger" title="Jolly Roger">Jolly Roger</a> emblem, meant for his infamous <b>MH5</b> shell.</li></ul>
<p>Finally, the armor features two segmented arm-guards made of plainer steel<span style="font-weight: normal"> (<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja">鋼</span><span class="t_nihongo_comma">,</span> <i><span class="t_nihongo_romaji">Hagane</span></i><span class="t_nihongo_help"><sup><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Help:Japanese" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Help:Japanese"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color:#00e;font:bold 80% sans-serif;text-decoration:none;padding:0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup></span>)</span>, which Krieg can raise over his face at a moment's notice. These also boast built-in armaments:
</p>
<ul><li>The right holds a small flamethrower with considerable range, capable of reducing a log to cinders within seconds.<sup id="cite_ref-18" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-18">&#91;18&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li>The left can deploy a weighted metal net for entangling enemies.<sup id="cite_ref-19" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-19">&#91;19&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="MH5">MH5</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FKrieg%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D19&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h5>
<dl><dd><i>Further information: <a href="/wiki/MH5" title="MH5">MH5</a></i></dd></dl>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/d1/MH5.png/revision/latest?cb=20230320023001" class="image"><img alt="MH5" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="141" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="MH5.png" data-image-key="MH5.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/d1/MH5.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20230320023001" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/d1/MH5.png/revision/latest?cb=20230320023001" class="image"><img alt="MH5" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/d1/MH5.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20230320023001" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="141" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="MH5.png" data-image-key="MH5.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/d1/MH5.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20230320023001" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:MH5.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">The MH5</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>The deadly poison-gas bomb <b>MH5</b><span style="font-weight: normal"> (<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja">猛毒ガス弾 <ruby lang="ja"><rb>M・H・5</rb><rp>（</rp><rt>エム・エイチ・ファイブ</rt><rp>）</rp></ruby></span><span class="t_nihongo_comma">,</span> <i><span class="t_nihongo_romaji">Mōdoku Gasu-Dan Emu-eichi-faibu</span></i><span class="t_nihongo_help"><sup><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Help:Japanese" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Help:Japanese"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color:#00e;font:bold 80% sans-serif;text-decoration:none;padding:0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup></span>)</span> is Krieg's most dreaded weapon: an <a href="/wiki/Explosive#Poison_Gas_Bombs" title="Explosive">explosive shell</a> containing a highly potent <a href="/wiki/Poison" title="Poison">chemical toxin</a>. Typically fired from the central launcher in Krieg's left shoulder-plate, its impact spreads a large cloud of gas that lasts around five minutes.<sup id="cite_ref-c62_20-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c62-20">&#91;20&#93;</a></sup> The poison inflicts immediate organ failure and internal bleeding on anyone who breathes it unprotected and, according to Krieg, kills within an hour.
</p><p>As a precaution for its use, Krieg and his crewmen all carry gas masks. The gas is apparently harmless through mere skin exposure, as <a href="/wiki/Monkey_D._Luffy" title="Monkey D. Luffy">Luffy</a>—with a stolen mask—was able to survive with no ill effects even when his body was completely engulfed.
</p><p>Knowing it can destroy whole villages, Krieg uses this weapon sparingly. In fact, he has been known to bait enemies with a decoy that looks identical to the real shell, but explodes to scatter <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/shuriken" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:shuriken">shuriken</a> instead.<sup id="cite_ref-21" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-21">&#91;21&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Daisenso">Daisenso</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FKrieg%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D20&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h5>
<dl><dd><i>Further information: <a href="/wiki/Daisenso" title="Daisenso">Daisenso</a></i></dd></dl>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/2/2b/Daisenso_Infobox.png/revision/latest?cb=20221124152203" class="image"><img alt="Daisenso Infobox" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="135" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Daisenso Infobox.png" data-image-key="Daisenso_Infobox.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/2/2b/Daisenso_Infobox.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20221124152203" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/2/2b/Daisenso_Infobox.png/revision/latest?cb=20221124152203" class="image"><img alt="Daisenso Infobox" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/2/2b/Daisenso_Infobox.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20221124152203" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="135" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Daisenso Infobox.png" data-image-key="Daisenso_Infobox.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/2/2b/Daisenso_Infobox.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20221124152203" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Daisenso_Infobox.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Krieg's signature weapon, the Daisenso.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>The <b>Daisenso</b><span style="font-weight: normal"> (<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja">大戦槍</span><span class="t_nihongo_comma">,</span> <i><span class="t_nihongo_romaji">Daisensō</span></i><span class="t_nihongo_help"><sup><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Help:Japanese" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Help:Japanese"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color:#00e;font:bold 80% sans-serif;text-decoration:none;padding:0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup></span>, literally meaning "Battle Spear")</span> is Krieg's ultimate melee weapon, formed by locking his shoulder-plates against one another and activating internal devices that produce a shaft and a blade from between.<sup id="cite_ref-c64_22-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c64-22">&#91;22&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>In addition to its long reach, the spear's head explodes on impact with any solid surface, with heavier impacts producing proportionally larger explosions; thus, even glancing hits or near-misses can wreak severe damage. To compensate for the blade's relative fragility, the explosive mechanism is stored primarily in the plates, allowing the spear to keep exploding even if the blade is completely destroyed.<sup id="cite_ref-23" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-23">&#91;23&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Gauntlets">Gauntlets</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FKrieg%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D21&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Beneath his gloves, Krieg wears a set of <b>diamond fists</b><span style="font-weight: normal"> (<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja">ダイヤの拳</span><span class="t_nihongo_comma">,</span> <i><span class="t_nihongo_romaji">Daiya no Kobushi</span></i><span class="t_nihongo_help"><sup><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Help:Japanese" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Help:Japanese"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color:#00e;font:bold 80% sans-serif;text-decoration:none;padding:0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup></span>)</span>, metal gauntlets with a small diamond over each knuckle and a larger one on the back of each hand.<sup id="cite_ref-c47_17-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c47-17">&#91;17&#93;</a></sup> Combined with Krieg's natural strength, these can shatter a full-sized mast in one blow.<sup id="cite_ref-24" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-24">&#91;24&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Kenzan_Mantle">Kenzan Mantle</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FKrieg%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D22&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>The <b><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kenzan" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Kenzan">Kenzan</a> Mantle</b><span style="font-weight: normal"> (<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja">剣山マント</span><span class="t_nihongo_comma">,</span> <i><span class="t_nihongo_romaji">Kenzan Manto</span></i><span class="t_nihongo_help"><sup><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Help:Japanese" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Help:Japanese"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color:#00e;font:bold 80% sans-serif;text-decoration:none;padding:0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup></span>, lit. "Sword Mountain Mantle"; <b>Porcupine Cape</b> in all English versions)</span> is a secondary cape covered with fist-sized metal spikes. Normally stored under one of Krieg's shoulder-plates, it is used as a defense in close quarters, especially against foes that try to aim for his legs or head.<sup id="cite_ref-c63_25-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c63-25">&#91;25&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Other_Weapons">Other Weapons</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FKrieg%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D23&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/0/07/Tetsu_no_Ame.png/revision/latest?cb=20230524234902" class="image"><img alt="Tetsu no Ame" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="179" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Tetsu no Ame.png" data-image-key="Tetsu_no_Ame.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/0/07/Tetsu_no_Ame.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230524234902" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/0/07/Tetsu_no_Ame.png/revision/latest?cb=20230524234902" class="image"><img alt="Tetsu no Ame" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/0/07/Tetsu_no_Ame.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230524234902" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="179" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Tetsu no Ame.png" data-image-key="Tetsu_no_Ame.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/0/07/Tetsu_no_Ame.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230524234902" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Tetsu_no_Ame.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Krieg using Tetsu no Ame.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Krieg carries at least two double-barreled <a href="/wiki/Firearm#Pistol" title="Firearm">pistols</a> on his person. Used in conjunction with his armor's gun array, these bring his maximum rate of fire to fourteen rounds per second.
</p><p>During the first part of his battle against Luffy, he wielded a huge spiked flail on a chain, apparently unconnected to any part of his armor.<sup id="cite_ref-26" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-26">&#91;26&#93;</a></sup> While reasonably effective, Krieg apparently abandoned it after Luffy deflected it, temporarily knocking out <a href="/wiki/Pearl" title="Pearl">Pearl</a>.
</p><p>Also separate from his armor, Krieg carries a number of marble-sized bombs that can create powerful explosions even if thrown by hand. Krieg commonly scatters them in large numbers to destabilize the battlefield in his favor.<sup id="cite_ref-27" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-27">&#91;27&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p><a href="/wiki/Carne" title="Carne">Carne</a>'s account of Krieg's origins shows him with a <a href="/wiki/Sword" title="Sword">sword</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-c46p17_6-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c46p17-6">&#91;6&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Video_Game_Only_Techniques">Video Game Only Techniques</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FKrieg%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D24&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul><li><b>Krieg Kantai Delta Explosion</b><span style="font-weight: normal"> (<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja">クリーク艦隊・デルタエクスプロージョン</span><span class="t_nihongo_comma">,</span> <i><span class="t_nihongo_romaji">Kurīku Kantai Deruta Ekusupurōjon</span></i><span class="t_nihongo_help"><sup><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Help:Japanese" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Help:Japanese"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color:#00e;font:bold 80% sans-serif;text-decoration:none;padding:0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup></span>, literally meaning "Krieg Fleet Delta Explosion")</span>: Working in tandem with <a href="/wiki/Gin" title="Gin">Gin</a> and <a href="/wiki/Pearl" title="Pearl">Pearl</a>, the three charge an opponent simultaneously. Gin strikes with his tonfa, Krieg with his Daisenso, and Pearl with one of his handheld shields. This attack can focus on a single enemy or damage multiple enemies at once. The technique appears in <i><a href="/wiki/One_Piece_Treasure_Cruise" title="One Piece Treasure Cruise">One Piece Treasure Cruise</a></i>.</li></ul>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="History">History</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FKrieg%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D25&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Past">Past</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FKrieg%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D26&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="The_Beginning">The Beginning</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FKrieg%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D27&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>When he was first starting out as a <a href="/wiki/Pirate" title="Pirate">pirate</a>, Krieg was a prisoner who&#160;took over&#160;a <a href="/wiki/Marine_Ships" title="Marine Ships">Marine ship</a> by posing as an Marine&#160;and&#160;killing its <a href="/wiki/Marine_Ranks#Commissioned_Marine_Officers" title="Marine Ranks">commanding officer</a>.&#160;He was also known to raid&#160;towns and passenger <a href="/wiki/Ship" title="Ship">ships</a>&#160;under the guise of a Marine flag and attacked his enemies under a white flag, both&#160;without raising suspicion. Krieg's crooked methods and drive to win&#160;enabled him to build his <a href="/wiki/Krieg_Pirates" title="Krieg Pirates">crew</a> into the largest&#160;<a href="/wiki/Fleet" title="Fleet">armada</a> of pirates in <a href="/wiki/East_Blue" title="East Blue">East Blue</a>&#160;at the time,&#160;giving&#160;him the title, "Pirate Admiral Don Krieg".<sup id="cite_ref-c46p17_6-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c46p17-6">&#91;6&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Attempt_to_Conquer_the_Grand_Line">Attempt to Conquer the Grand Line</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FKrieg%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D28&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 200px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/b/b8/Krieg_Pirates_Return_from_Grand_Line.png/revision/latest?cb=20221124191313" class="image"><img alt="Krieg Pirates Return from Grand Line" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="200" height="150" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Krieg Pirates Return from Grand Line.png" data-image-key="Krieg_Pirates_Return_from_Grand_Line.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/b/b8/Krieg_Pirates_Return_from_Grand_Line.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20221124191313" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/b/b8/Krieg_Pirates_Return_from_Grand_Line.png/revision/latest?cb=20221124191313" class="image"><img alt="Krieg Pirates Return from Grand Line" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/b/b8/Krieg_Pirates_Return_from_Grand_Line.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20221124191313" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="200" height="150" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Krieg Pirates Return from Grand Line.png" data-image-key="Krieg_Pirates_Return_from_Grand_Line.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/b/b8/Krieg_Pirates_Return_from_Grand_Line.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20221124191313" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Krieg_Pirates_Return_from_Grand_Line.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Gin posing as Krieg to lure Fullbody away.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Krieg made a trip to the <a href="/wiki/Grand_Line" title="Grand Line">Grand Line</a> with his fleet, hoping to find the <a href="/wiki/One_Piece" title="One Piece">One Piece</a> and become the next Pirate King. However, on his seventh day in the Grand Line, he ran afoul with <a href="/wiki/Dracule_Mihawk" title="Dracule Mihawk">Dracule Mihawk</a>, one of the <a href="/wiki/Seven_Warlords_of_the_Sea" title="Seven Warlords of the Sea">Seven Warlords of the Sea</a> who completely decimated his fleet. With only one ship escaping through sheer luck but in terrible condition, Krieg returned defeated to the <a href="/wiki/East_Blue" title="East Blue">East Blue</a>.
</p><p>He then had his right hand man, <a href="/wiki/Gin" title="Gin">Gin</a>, disguise himself as the Pirate Admiral and act as a decoy in order to lure away the Marine ship that had <a href="/wiki/Marine_Ranks#Lieutenant" title="Marine Ranks">Lieutenant</a> <a href="/wiki/Fullbody" title="Fullbody">Fullbody</a> on it, in order to save the remaining members of the severely exhausted crew.<br style="clear:both;" />
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="East_Blue_Saga">East Blue Saga</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FKrieg%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D29&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Baratie_Arc">Baratie Arc</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FKrieg%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D30&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Gin made it back to the crew and told his boss, Krieg, that he could take the crew to the Baratie.<sup id="cite_ref-c45_1-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c45-1">&#91;1&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Two days later, Krieg and his crew arrived at the Baratie with his <a href="/wiki/Dreadnaught_Sabre" title="Dreadnaught Sabre">ship</a>. The chefs and clients were at first terrorized because of Krieg's terrible reputation. However, it quickly appeared that the ship was in a pitiful shape and it was an agonizing Krieg that entered the restaurant with the support of Gin.
</p><p>After Krieg and Gin entered the restaurant, everyone was shocked that Krieg was begging for food and water. Krieg then fell to the floor and Gin begged them to help his captain but <a href="/wiki/Patty" title="Patty">Patty</a> laughed at him. Gin continuously begged for food, saying they had money to pay and that made them their customers. Patty denied them and the other chefs commented on how dreadful Krieg really was. Krieg then bowed his head and begged for food. Gin stopped him and was seen crying.
</p><p>Sanji arrived with food and kicked Patty out of the way. All of them were shocked that Sanji was offering food to Krieg. Krieg quickly devoured the food, and after he finished eating, he attacked Sanji immediately and Gin was shocked by his captain's actions. Krieg broke Gin's shoulder and the customers evacuated the restaurant in a panic.
</p><p>Krieg gazed at the whole restaurant and said that he liked it. He explained that his ship was battered and wanted the Baratie as its replacement. He also demanded food for his crew as to which the chefs refused. He explained that he was not ordering food, and that he was giving them an order. Krieg roared and said that nobody has ever disobeyed him.<sup id="cite_ref-28" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-28">&#91;28&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/0/0f/Zeff_Gives_Krieg_Food.png/revision/latest?cb=20220523013146" class="image"><img alt="Zeff Gives Krieg Food" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="155" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Zeff Gives Krieg Food.png" data-image-key="Zeff_Gives_Krieg_Food.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/0/0f/Zeff_Gives_Krieg_Food.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20220523013146" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/0/0f/Zeff_Gives_Krieg_Food.png/revision/latest?cb=20220523013146" class="image"><img alt="Zeff Gives Krieg Food" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/0/0f/Zeff_Gives_Krieg_Food.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20220523013146" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="155" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Zeff Gives Krieg Food.png" data-image-key="Zeff_Gives_Krieg_Food.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/0/0f/Zeff_Gives_Krieg_Food.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20220523013146" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Zeff_Gives_Krieg_Food.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Krieg meets with Zeff.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Before Sanji went to prepare food for Krieg's crew, Patty smashed him into the floor and offered Krieg a dessert and brought out a cannon and attacked Krieg with Shokuatari Meatball. Krieg complained how awful the dessert was and revealed his arsenal of weapons and began attacking the chefs. Krieg explained why he was the strongest before Zeff brought food for a hundred people. However, upon hearing Zeff's name, Krieg was shocked.<sup id="cite_ref-c47_17-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c47-17">&#91;17&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Krieg told the story of Zeff the Red Leg, who was supposed to have died in an accident, but he only lost a leg which made him unable to fight anymore and forced him to retire from his career as a pirate and became the chef of a restaurant. Since Zeff once went to the Grand Line and returned safely, Krieg wanted the <a href="/wiki/Logbook#Zeff&#39;s_Logbook" title="Logbook">logbook</a> written at that time. However, he would have to take it by force since Zeff decided not to lend it, given his feelings to the remnant of his former life.<sup id="cite_ref-c48_15-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c48-15">&#91;15&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Krieg then left the restaurant to feed his crew, leaving the chefs the choice to flee or die. After returning to his ship, Krieg gave the food to his crew, enabling them to recover. Krieg told them of his plan to steal the Baratie ship and return to the Grand Line. When he saw the lack of motivation in his men to return to that place, he shot the man who criticized his decision, which appeared to quickly change their mind. When they started attacking the restaurant, their galleon was suddenly cut in half. They then saw that the Warlord of the Sea Dracule Mihawk had followed the Krieg Pirates all the way to East Blue.<sup id="cite_ref-29" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-29">&#91;29&#93;</a></sup> After Zoro was defeated by Mihawk,<sup id="cite_ref-30" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-30">&#91;30&#93;</a></sup> Krieg tried to attack him, only to be completely ignored. Mihawk sliced the galleon once more before departing. The Krieg pirates resumed their attack on the Baratie.<sup id="cite_ref-31" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-31">&#91;31&#93;</a></sup> Krieg wanted to take over the ship so that they could travel more incognito, in addition to taking Zeff's logbook so that they could learn about the powers of Grand Line and how to fight them. However, the chefs were ready to fight and they released a wood platform in front of the restaurant so that they did not have to fight inside the restaurant and damage it. Patty and Carne drove a secret weapon hidden in the fish head of the Baratie, but Krieg got rid of it easily and threw it back toward the chefs, but Sanji kicked it back just as easily, showing his true strength.<sup id="cite_ref-32" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-32">&#91;32&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>While Luffy was watching Sanji’s fight against <a href="/wiki/Pearl" title="Pearl">Pearl</a>, Krieg treacherously attacked Luffy. Luffy was tossed into the back of Pearl's head, forcing Pearl to smash his face against his own armor.<sup id="cite_ref-33" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-33">&#91;33&#93;</a></sup> In order to stop a berserk Pearl from destroying the ship he was after, Krieg threw a knob toward Sanji and Pearl but Luffy was able to deflect it. The knob instead destroyed Krieg's ship mast which, by falling, knocked out Pearl. However, the Krieg Pirates had not said their last word. While they were fighting, Gin took Zeff down and was threatening his life with a gun.<sup id="cite_ref-c55_13-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c55-13">&#91;13&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>When Krieg asked Luffy the question of who was stronger, Luffy naturally said that he was the stronger one there. In order to make him realize the difference between the two of them, Krieg threatened Luffy with one of his strongest weapon: poison gas MH5. When Luffy tried to bounce it back, it was revealed to be a shuriken bomb. Luffy admitted that he was tricked, but continued to say he was the strongest. As his anger rose, Krieg asked Gin to take care of Sanji, while he would deal with Luffy personally.<sup id="cite_ref-34" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-34">&#91;34&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Luffy tried to attack Krieg, but Krieg shot Luffy with bombs and spears. The spears harmed Luffy at his foot, and he almost fell into ocean. Luffy then asked if Krieg was serious in fighting with him. Krieg answered that the important thing in fighting was strategy to kill the opponent. Krieg said that Luffy was a monkey because he just attacks without strategy.<sup id="cite_ref-35" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-35">&#91;35&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>When Gin refused to kill Sanji because he helped him, Krieg was disappointed with Gin because he was the person whom he trusted the most. Gin requested to let the Baratie go, angering Krieg. Because of that, Krieg planned to shoot MH5 poison gas. Not seeing Gin as his crewmate, Krieg demanded that he throw away his mask. Meanwhile, Luffy tried to stop Krieg, but he did not succeed. Gin threw away his mask before Krieg unleashed his MH5. The Baratie's chefs escaped by diving and Krieg's crew used their masks. After five minutes, the gas dispersed and it was revealed that Gin gave Luffy his mask. Krieg angered Luffy and Sanji by saying that Gin was garbage and it was proper for him to die by his own hands as his commander.<sup id="cite_ref-c62_20-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c62-20">&#91;20&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Luffy was really angry at Krieg and said that Gin may not die and had to survive. However, because of the poison, Gin would die in one hour. Luffy promised to defeat Krieg and started his attack at Krieg's front. Krieg affronted if he was more foolish than a monkey, because monkeys will not challenge people who are impossible to beat. Luffy replied by saying that he is a monkey who does not know the word of surrender.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/d0/Luffy_Hits_Krieg_With_Gomu_Gomu_no_Bullet.png/revision/latest?cb=20230320023202" class="image"><img alt="Luffy Hits Krieg With Gomu Gomu no Bullet" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Luffy Hits Krieg With Gomu Gomu no Bullet.png" data-image-key="Luffy_Hits_Krieg_With_Gomu_Gomu_no_Bullet.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/d0/Luffy_Hits_Krieg_With_Gomu_Gomu_no_Bullet.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230320023202" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/d0/Luffy_Hits_Krieg_With_Gomu_Gomu_no_Bullet.png/revision/latest?cb=20230320023202" class="image"><img alt="Luffy Hits Krieg With Gomu Gomu no Bullet" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/d0/Luffy_Hits_Krieg_With_Gomu_Gomu_no_Bullet.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230320023202" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Luffy Hits Krieg With Gomu Gomu no Bullet.png" data-image-key="Luffy_Hits_Krieg_With_Gomu_Gomu_no_Bullet.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/d0/Luffy_Hits_Krieg_With_Gomu_Gomu_no_Bullet.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230320023202" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Luffy_Hits_Krieg_With_Gomu_Gomu_no_Bullet.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Luffy hits Krieg.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Krieg attacked with a hail of spears fired from his weapon. Luffy, without hesitation, ran straight into the attack with the intent of reaching Krieg. Realizing the rookie pirate wasn't stopping, Krieg revealed a robe made of dangerous spikes to deter any attacks. However, to the surprise of everyone, Luffy still attacked despite the injury inflicted to his hand, knocking Krieg to the ground.
</p><p>Standing back up, Krieg revealed his final weapon, a large spear with an explosive end that detonates upon impact. Continuing the battle, the surrounding wreckage was eventually reduced to sunken rubble, with both combatants having very little room to move on. Determined, Luffy began striking the spear itself, and eventually broke the end. Grinning with confidence, Luffy told Krieg to prepare himself.<sup id="cite_ref-c63_25-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c63-25">&#91;25&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Krieg was knocked down once again by Luffy. When one of Krieg's crewmates stated that he believed Luffy to actually be stronger than Krieg, he arose, telling them to shut up before combining his shoulder plates together to form his "Giant Battle Spear", which he slammed into the ground next to Luffy, creating an explosion.
</p><p>While Luffy wondered how the spear made an explosion, Krieg swung it again, sending Luffy flying over the ocean, but luckily, he stretched towards a platform floating. However, due to the fact that he had lost lots of blood thanks to Krieg, and that the platform he was standing on was unstable, he soon fell to his knees. Krieg continued his assault on Luffy, who was dodging for his life.
</p><p>Finally, Luffy lost balance and jumped over Krieg's blow, but this made him wide open for an attack. However, just in the nick of time, Luffy grabbed the lance before it could hit him. Enraged, Krieg slammed the lance into the ground, forcing Luffy to let go. Krieg proceeded to ram his lance into Luffy, who grabbed the tip, but Krieg merely whipped it around, creating an explosion which sent Luffy flying. As Krieg swung again, Luffy was hit head-on. Krieg then proceeded to tell that he was stronger than Luffy.
</p><p>However, Luffy answered by slamming his foot into the ground, breaking the spear's tip, much to Krieg's confusion and horror. Luffy told him that he hit the tip five times, and that with the wide area they had landed in, Luffy could beat him.<sup id="cite_ref-c64_22-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c64-22">&#91;22&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Luffy_Breaks_Krieg%27s_Armor_With_Gomu_Gomu_No_Bazooka.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Luffy breaks Krieg's armor.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Krieg attacked Luffy again and wanted to execute him because he was brave to challenge "The Most Powerful Captain" in East Blue. Luffy dodged the attack and hanged onto a mast. Krieg then sliced the mast, but his attacks did not hurt Luffy. Luffy threw the mast at him, but Krieg destroyed it by shooting fire at it. Luffy countered with a "Gomu Gomu no Gatling", but Krieg's armor protected him. Luffy continued by trying "Gomu Gomu no Pistol" and sent Krieg flying, but the armor still did not break. Krieg planned to throw bombs from top of the mast. Luffy tried to stop him and ran faster. Finally, he destroyed the armor by using "Gomu Gomu no Bazooka" and made it crack into pieces.<sup id="cite_ref-36" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-36">&#91;36&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Even though Krieg lost his spirit, he attacked Luffy in the air by shooting an iron net at him. Unfortunately for Luffy, he was trapped in it and below them was the ocean. If still in that condition, Luffy would sink, and because of that, Krieg was really satisfied. However, Luffy planned to use his hands and feet for one last attack. Anticipating Luffy's next move, Krieg ordered his crew to shoot at Luffy, but they were stopped by Sanji. Luffy was successful in using "<a href="/wiki/Gomu_Gomu_no_Mi/Techniques" title="Gomu Gomu no Mi/Techniques">Gomu Gomu no Ozuchi</a>", smashing Krieg's head into the dock, causing him to lose consciousness. After losing the battle, Krieg stood up again and went berserk. Before he could continue, Gin punched Krieg in the stomach. Gin then departed the Baratie with Krieg and the rest of his crew.<sup id="cite_ref-37" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-37">&#91;37&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Final_Saga">Final Saga</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FKrieg%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D31&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Egghead_Arc">Egghead Arc</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FKrieg%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D32&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Two years later, on <a href="/wiki/Hachinosu" title="Hachinosu">Hachinosu</a>, Krieg walked alongside Gin during <a href="/wiki/Vegapunk" title="Vegapunk">Vegapunk</a>'s broadcast.<sup id="cite_ref-38" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-38">&#91;38&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Major_Battles">Major Battles</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FKrieg%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D33&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<ul><li>Krieg vs. a <a href="/wiki/Marine_Ranks#Commissioned_Marine_Officers" title="Marine Ranks">commanding officer</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Krieg_Pirates" title="Krieg Pirates">Krieg Pirates</a> vs. <a href="/wiki/Dracule_Mihawk" title="Dracule Mihawk">Dracule Mihawk</a></li>
