<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Adaptation_Differences">Adaptation Differences</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FKrieg%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D34&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>In the manga, Krieg's hair has a deep blue color, as opposed to its purple hue in the anime.
</p><p>For unknown reasons, the anime does not depict Krieg's shuriken bomb, making his threat to deploy the MH5 a serious one from the start.
</p><p>In the <a href="/wiki/One_Piece_(Live-Action_Series)" title="One Piece (Live-Action Series)">live-action series</a>, Krieg does not survive his battle with <a href="/wiki/Dracule_Mihawk" title="Dracule Mihawk">Dracule Mihawk</a> and so does not show up at the <a href="/wiki/Baratie" title="Baratie">Baratie</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-39" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-39">&#91;39&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Translation_and_Dub_Issues">Translation and Dub Issues</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FKrieg%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D35&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Name_and_Title">Name and Title</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FKrieg%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D36&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><i><a href="https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/Krieg" class="extiw" title="wiktionary:Krieg">Krieg</a></i> is German for "war", alluding to Krieg's heavy arsenal and massive naval fleet.<sup id="cite_ref-40" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-40">&#91;40&#93;</a></sup> In German translations of the series, it is rendered as <i>Creek</i>.
</p><p>Additionally, while Krieg's "Teitoku"<span style="font-weight: normal"> (<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja">提督</span><span class="t_nihongo_help"><sup><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Help:Japanese" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Help:Japanese"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color:#00e;font:bold 80% sans-serif;text-decoration:none;padding:0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup></span>)</span> epithet is rendered as "Admiral" by both the <a href="/wiki/4Kids_Entertainment" title="4Kids Entertainment">4Kids</a>-dubbed anime and the <a href="/wiki/VIZ_Media" title="VIZ Media">VIZ</a> manga, it should be noted that the term is <i>not</i> the one used for the <a href="/wiki/Marines" title="Marines">Marines</a>' "<a href="/wiki/Admiral" title="Admiral">Admiral</a>"<span style="font-weight: normal"> (<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja">大将</span><span class="t_nihongo_comma">,</span> <i><span class="t_nihongo_romaji">Taishō</span></i><span class="t_nihongo_help"><sup><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Help:Japanese" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Help:Japanese"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color:#00e;font:bold 80% sans-serif;text-decoration:none;padding:0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup></span>)</span> rank. The <a href="/wiki/Funimation" title="Funimation">Funimation</a> anime instead translates it as "Commodore"—a convention it would later use for the anime-original <a href="/wiki/Nelson_Royale" title="Nelson Royale">Nelson Royale</a>.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Weaponry">Weaponry</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FKrieg%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D37&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Due to its general policy against graphic violence and bloodshed, <a href="/wiki/4Kids_Entertainment" title="4Kids Entertainment">4Kids</a> digitally edited Krieg's Gatling gun spears into "poison suction cups" (presumably smeared with contact poison). Curiously, this edit only applied to the spears after they had struck Luffy; the initial scenes of Krieg firing them were left unaltered.
</p><p>On the same principle, <a href="/wiki/4Kids_Entertainment" title="4Kids Entertainment">4Kids</a> also recolored Krieg's pistols to appear more toy-like, though most of the firing animations were left unchanged.
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Early_Concepts">Early Concepts</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FKrieg%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D38&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/c/cb/Early_Don_Krieg.png/revision/latest?cb=20150404102114" class="image"><img alt="Early Don Krieg" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="323" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Early Don Krieg.png" data-image-key="Early_Don_Krieg.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/c/cb/Early_Don_Krieg.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20150404102114" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/c/cb/Early_Don_Krieg.png/revision/latest?cb=20150404102114" class="image"><img alt="Early Don Krieg" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/c/cb/Early_Don_Krieg.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20150404102114" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="323" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Early Don Krieg.png" data-image-key="Early_Don_Krieg.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/c/cb/Early_Don_Krieg.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20150404102114" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Early_Don_Krieg.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Early concept of Krieg in <i>One Piece Green</i>.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p><i><a href="/wiki/One_Piece_Green:_Secret_Pieces" title="One Piece Green: Secret Pieces">One Piece Green: Secret Pieces</a></i> revealed an early concept-draft of Krieg, depicting him as a cyborg named "Krieg - 9000".<br style="clear:both;" />
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Merchandise">Merchandise</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FKrieg%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D39&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>

<ul><li><i><a href="/wiki/Grand_Battle!_Swan_Colosseum" title="Grand Battle! Swan Colosseum">Grand Battle! Swan Colosseum</a></i></li></ul>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Trivia">Trivia</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FKrieg%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D45&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<ul><li>In the first version of Opening 1, Krieg's hair was shown as long, causing confusion among fans. It was later revealed this look was taken from his wanted poster, rather than his more recent appearance.</li>
<li>He shares the same Japanese dub voice actor with <a href="/wiki/Sakazuki" title="Sakazuki">Sakazuki</a>, and the same Funimation dub voice actor with <a href="/wiki/Wapol" title="Wapol">Wapol</a>.</li>
<li>Krieg is the first antagonist in the series to mention <a href="/wiki/One_Piece" title="One Piece">One Piece</a>, and be depicted with open ambitions of being the <a href="/wiki/Pirate#Pirate_King" title="Pirate">Pirate King</a>.</li>
<li>Krieg's favorite food is roasted whole <a href="/wiki/Sea_King" title="Sea King">Sea King</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-vivre_card_3-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-vivre_card-3">&#91;3&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li>Krieg's name means "war" in German, which is probably a reference to his warmongering behavior.</li></ul>
